Create a user\n            user = User(username='testuser', role_id=admin_role.id)\n            user.set_password('testpass')\n            db.session.add(user)\n            db.session.commit()\n            self.user_id = user.id\n            self.admin_role_id = admin_role.id\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.session.remove()\n            db.drop_all()\n\n    def login(self, username='testuser', password='testpass'):\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/login', json={'username': username, 'password': password})\n        return rv\n\n    def logout(self):\n        return self.app.post('/api/logout')\n\n    def register_user(self, username, password, role_id=None):\n        data = {'username': username, 'password': password}\n        if role_id:\n            data['role_id'] = role_id\n        return self.app.post('/api/register', json=data)\n\n    def test_user_registration_and_login_logout(self):\n        # Register new user\n        rv = self.register_user('newuser', 'newpass', self.admin_role_id)\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'User registered successfully', rv.data)\n\n        # Duplicate username\n        rv = self.register_user('newuser', 'newpass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(b'Username already exists', rv.data)\n\n        # Login\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/login', json={'username': 'newuser', 'password': 'newpass'})\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Logged in', rv.data)\n\n        # Wrong password\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/login', json={'username': 'newuser', 'password': 'wrongpass'})\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 401)\n        self.assertIn(b'Invalid credentials', rv.data)\n\n        # Logout (should fail if not logged in)\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/logout')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 401)\n\n    def test_roles_list(self):\n        self.login()\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/roles')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        data = rv.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(r['name'] == 'admin' for r in data))\n        self.assertTrue(any(r['name'] == 'accountant' for r in data))\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_inventory_crud(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add inventory item\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json={\n            'name': 'Laptop',\n            'sku': 'LAP123',\n            'quantity': 10,\n            'cost': 500.0,\n            'price': 700.0\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Item added', rv.data)\n\n        # Duplicate SKU should succeed (not checked in code)\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json={\n            'name': 'Laptop 2',\n            'sku': 'LAP123',\n            'quantity': 5,\n            'cost': 400.0,\n            'price': 650.0\n        })\n        # Should fail due to unique constraint, but SQLAlchemy will raise an IntegrityError\n        # We cannot catch it here as the code does not handle it, so it will 500.\n        self.assertIn(rv.status_code, (400, 500))\n\n        # List inventory\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/inventory')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        data = rv.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(item['name'] == 'Laptop' for item in data))\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_ledger_entry(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add ledger entry\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/ledger', json={\n            'date': '2023-01-01',\n            'account': 'Cash',\n            'description': 'Initial balance',\n            'debit': 1000,\n            'credit': 0\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Entry added', rv.data)\n\n        # List ledger entries\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/ledger')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        data = rv.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(entry['account'] == 'Cash' for entry in data))\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_ledger_summary(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Get inventory item id\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/inventory')\n        data = rv.get_json()\n        monitor = next(item for item in data if item['sku'] == 'MON123')\n        monitor_id = monitor['id']\n\n        # Add purchase\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/purchases', json={\n            'date': '2023-01-10',\n            'supplier': 'SupplierA',\n            'total': 300.0,\n            'items': [\n                {'inventory_item_id': monitor_id, 'quantity': 3, 'cost': 100.0}\n            ]\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Purchase recorded', rv.data)\n\n        # Check inventory updated\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/inventory')\n        data = rv.get_json()\n        monitor = next(item for item in data if item['sku'] == 'MON123')\n        self.assertEqual(monitor['quantity'], 8)\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_invoices_and_inventory_update(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Get inventory item id\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/inventory')\n        data = rv.get_json()\n        keyboard = next(item for item in data if item['sku'] == 'KEY123')\n        keyboard_id = keyboard['id']\n\n        #                         "import unittest\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom app import app, db, User, Role, InventoryItem, LedgerEntry, Purchase, PurchaseItem, Invoice, InvoiceItem\n\nclass AccountingSystemTestCase(unittest.TestCase):\n    @classmethod\n    def setUpClass(cls):\n        # Use an in-memory SQLite database for testing\n        app.config['SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URI'] = 'sqlite:///:memory:'\n        app.config['TESTING'] = True\n        app.config['WTF_CSRF_ENABLED'] = False\n        app.config['LOGIN_DISABLED'] = False\n        cls.app = app.test_client()\n        cls.app_ctx = app.app_context()\n        cls.app_ctx.push()\n        db.create_all()\n        # Create roles\n        admin_role = Role(name='admin')\n        accountant_role = Role(name='accountant')\n        manager_role = Role(name='manager')\n        db.session.add_all([admin_role, accountant_role, manager_role])\n        db.session.commit()\n        # Create a default user\n        cls.admin = User(username='admin', role_id=admin_role.id)\n        cls.admin.set_password('password')\n        db.session.add(cls.admin)\n        db.session.commit()\n\n    @classmethod\n    def tearDownClass(cls):\n        db.session.remove()\n        db.drop_all()\n        cls.app_ctx.pop()\n\n    def login(self, username, password):\n        return self.app.post('/api/login', json={\n            'username': username,\n            'password': password\n        })\n\n    def logout(self):\n        return self.app.post('/api/logout')\n\n    def test_register_and_login_logout(self):\n        # Register a new user\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/register', json={\n            'username': 'testuser',\n            'password': 'testpass',\n            'role_id': Role.query.filter_by(name='accountant').first().id\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('User registered successfully', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Duplicate registration should fail\n        rv2 = self.app.post('/api/register', json={\n            'username': 'testuser',\n            'password': 'testpass'\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn('Username already exists', rv2.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Login with correct credentials\n        rv3 = self.login('testuser', 'testpass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Logged in', rv3.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Login with wrong password\n        rv4 = self.login('testuser', 'wrongpass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv4.status_code, 401)\n        self.assertIn('Invalid credentials', rv4.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Logout\n        rv5 = self.logout()\n        self.assertEqual(rv5.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Logged out', rv5.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n    def test_roles_endpoint(self):\n        self.login('admin', 'password')\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/roles')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        data = rv.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(role['name'] == 'admin' for role in data))\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_inventory_crud(self):\n        self.login('admin', 'password')\n        # Add another item with same SKU (should fail at DB level, but not handled here)\n        rv2 = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json={\n            'name': 'Laptop2',\n            'sku': 'SKU123',\n            'quantity': 5,\n            'cost': 300.0,\n            'price': 400.0\n        })\n        # Should raise IntegrityError, but endpoint doesn't catch it, so 500\n        self.assertIn(rv2.status_code, (400, 500))\n\n        # Get inventory\n        rv3 = self.app.get('/api/inventory')\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 200)\n        items = rv3.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(items), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(items[0]['name'], 'Laptop')\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_ledger_entry_and_report(self):\n        self.login('admin', 'password')\n        # Add ledger entry\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/ledger', json={\n            'date': '2024-06-01',\n            'account': 'Cash',\n            'description': 'Initial deposit',\n            'debit': 1000,\n            'credit': 0\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Entry added', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Add another entry\n        rv2 = self.app.post('/api/ledger', json={\n            'date': '2024-06-02',\n            'account': 'Sales',\n            'description': 'Sale of goods',\n            'debit': 0,\n            'credit': 500\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 200)\n\n        # Get ledger\n        rv3 = self.app.get('/api/ledger')\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 200)\n        entries = rv3.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(entries), 2)\n        self.assertEqual(entries[0]['account'], 'Sales')\n        self.assertEqual(entries[1]['account'], 'Cash')\n\n        # Ledger summary report\n        rv4 = self.app.get('/api/reports/ledger-summary')\n        self.assertEqual(rv4.status_code, 200)\n        summary = rv4.get_json()\n        accounts = {s['account']: s for s in summary}\n        self.assertEqual(accounts['Cash']['total_debit'], 1000.0)\n        self.assertEqual(accounts['Sales']['total_credit'], 500.0)\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_purchases_and_inventory_update(self):\n        self.login('admin', 'password')\n        # Add purchase\n        rv2 = self.app.post('/api/purchases', json={\n            'date': '2024-06-03',\n            'supplier': 'Supplier1',\n            'total': 500.0,\n            'items': [\n                {\n                    'inventory_item_id': item_id,\n                    'quantity': 10,\n                    'cost': 50.0\n                }\n            ]\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Purchase recorded', rv2.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Inventory should be updated\n        item = InventoryItem.query.get(item_id)\n        self.assertEqual(item.quantity, 15)\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_invoices_and_inventory_update(self):\n        self.login('admin', 'password')\n        # Add inventory item\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json={\n            'name': 'Keyboard',\n            'sku': 'SKU789',\n            'quantity': 20,\n            'cost': 20.0,\n            'price': 30.0\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        item_id = InventoryItem.query.filter_by(sku='SKU789').first().id\n\n        # Add invoice (sell 5 keyboards)\n        rv2 = self.app.post('/api/invoices', json={\n            'date': '2024-06-04',\n            'customer': 'Customer1',\n            'total': 150.0,\n            'items': [\n                {\n                    'inventory_item_id': item_id,\n                    'quantity': 5,\n                    'price': 30.0\n                }\n            ]\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Invoice recorded', rv2.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Inventory should be reduced\n        item = InventoryItem.query.get(item_id)\n        self.assertEqual(item.quantity, 15)\n\n        # Try to sell more than available (should allow, but inventory will go negative)\n        rv3 = self.app.post('/api/invoices', json={\n            'date': '2024-06-05',\n            'customer': 'Customer2',\n            'total': 600.0,\n            'items': [\n                {\n                    'inventory_item_id': item_id,\n                    'quantity': 20,\n                    'price': 30.0\n                }\n            ]\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 200)\n        item = InventoryItem.query.get(item_id)\n        self.assertEqual(item.quantity, -5)\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_auth_required(self):\n        # Try to access protected endpoint without login\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/ledger')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 401)\n\n        rv2 = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json={\n            'name': 'Mouse',\n            'sku': 'SKU999',\n            'quantity': 5,\n            'cost': 10.0,\n            'price': 15.0\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 401)\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    unittest.main()",
                        "import unittest\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom app import app, db, User, Role, InventoryItem, LedgerEntry, Purchase, PurchaseItem, Invoice, InvoiceItem\n\nclass AccountingSystemTestCase(unittest.TestCase):\n    @classmethod\n    def setUpClass(cls):\n        # Use SQLite in-memory DB for tests\n        app.config['SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URI'] = 'sqlite:///:memory:'\n        app.config['TESTING'] = True\n        app.config['WTF_CSRF_ENABLED'] = False\n        cls.app = app\n        cls.client = app.test_client()\n        with cls.app.app_context():\n            db.create_all()\n            # Create roles\n            admin_role = Role(name='admin')\n            accountant_role = Role(name='accountant')\n            db.session.add_all([admin_role, accountant_role])\n            db.session.commit()\n\n    @classmethod\n    def tearDownClass(cls):\n        with cls.app.app_context():\n            db.session.remove()\n            db.drop_all()\n\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.ctx = self.app.app_context()\n        self.ctx.push()\n        # Register a user and login for tests\n        self.username = 'testuser'\n        self.password = 'testpass'\n        self._register_user(self.username, self.password, role_id=1)\n        self._login_user(self.username, self.password)\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        self._logout_user()\n        # Clear all tables except roles\n        for tbl in [User, InventoryItem, LedgerEntry, Purchase, PurchaseItem, Invoice, InvoiceItem]:\n            db.session.query(tbl).delete()\n        db.session.commit()\n        self.ctx.pop()\n\n    # --- Helper functions ---\n    def _register_user(self, username, password, role_id=1):\n        return self.client.post('/api/register', json={\n            'username': username,\n            'password': password,\n            'role_id': role_id\n        })\n\n    def _login_user(self, username, password):\n        return self.client.post('/api/login', json={\n            'username': username,\n            'password': password\n        })\n\n    def _logout_user(self):\n        return self.client.post('/api/logout')\n\n    def _add_inventory_item(self, name, sku, quantity=0, cost=0, price=0):\n        return self.client.post('/api/inventory', json={\n            'name': name,\n            'sku': sku,\n            'quantity': quantity,\n            'cost': cost,\n            'price': price\n        })\n\n    # --- Tests ---\n\n    def test_register_duplicate_user(self):\n        resp = self._register_user(self.username, self.password)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn('Username already exists', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n    def test_login_logout(self):\n        # Correct credentials\n        resp = self._login_user(self.username, self.password)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Logged in', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n        # Logout\n        resp = self._logout_user()\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Logged out', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n        # Wrong credentials\n        resp = self._login_user(self.username, 'wrongpass')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 401)\n        self.assertIn('Invalid credentials', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n    def test_roles_list(self):\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/roles')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        data = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(r['name'] == 'admin' for r in data))\n\n    def test_inventory_crud(self):\n        # Add item\n        resp = self._add_inventory_item('Laptop', 'SKU123', 10, 500, 700)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Item added', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n        # List items\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/inventory')\n        items = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(items), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(items[0]['name'], 'Laptop')\n        # Add duplicate SKU (should fail)\n        resp = self._add_inventory_item('Monitor', 'SKU123')\n        self.assertNotEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n\n    def test_ledger_entry(self):\n        # Add ledger entry\n        payload = {\n            'date': '2024-01-01',\n            'account': 'Cash',\n            'description': 'Initial capital',\n            'debit': 1000,\n            'credit': 0\n        }\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/ledger', json=payload)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Entry added', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n        # List ledger entries\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/ledger')\n        entries = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(entries), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(entries[0]['account'], 'Cash')\n\n    def test_ledger_summary(self):\n        # Add multiple entries\n        self.client.post('/api/ledger', json={\n            'date': '2024-01-01',\n            'account': 'Cash',\n            'debit': 1000,\n            'credit': 0\n        })\n        self.client.post('/api/ledger', json={\n            'date': '2024-01-02',\n            'account': 'Cash',\n            'debit': 0,\n            'credit': 200\n        })\n        self.client.post('/api/ledger', json={\n            'date': '2024-01-03',\n            'account': 'Sales',\n            'debit': 0,\n            'credit': 500\n        })\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/reports/ledger-summary')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        summary = resp.get_json()\n        # Check for correct aggregation\n        cash = next((s for s in summary if s['account'] == 'Cash'), None)\n        sales = next((s for s in summary if s['account'] == 'Sales'), None)\n        self.assertIsNotNone(cash)\n        self.assertEqual(cash['total_debit'], 1000)\n        self.assertEqual(cash['total_credit'], 200)\n        self.assertIsNotNone(sales)\n        self.assertEqual(sales['total_credit'], 500)\n\n    def test_purchase_and_inventory_update(self):\n        # \"\"\"Purchase records\"\"\"\n    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)\n    date = db.Column(db.Date, nullable=False)\n    supplier = db.Column(db.String(128), nullable=False)\n    total = )\n            db.session.add(purchase)\n            db.session.flush()  # Get purchase.id before commit\n            for item in data['items']:\n                pi = PurchaseItem(\n      if current_user.role and current_user.role.name == role_name:\n                return func(*args, **kwargs)\n            return jsonify({'message': 'Access denied'}), 403\n                         "import unittest\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom app import app, db, User, Role, InventoryItem, LedgerEntry, Purchase, PurchaseItem, Invoice, InvoiceItem\n\nclass AccountingSystemTestCase(unittest.TestCase):\n    @classmethod\n    def setUpClass(cls):\n        # Use an in-memory SQLite database for testing\n        app.config['SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URI'] = 'sqlite:///:memory:'\n        app.config['TESTING'] = True\n        app.config['WTF_CSRF_ENABLED'] = False\n        cls.client = app.test_client()\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.create_all()\n            # Create roles\n            admin_role = Role(name='admin')\n            accountant_role = Role(name='accountant')\n            db.session.add_all([admin_role, accountant_role])\n            db.session.commit()\n            # Create a default admin user\n            user = User(username='admin', role_id=admin_role.id)\n            user.set_password('adminpass')\n            db.session.add(user)\n            db.session.commit()\n            cls.admin_user = user\n\n    @classmethod\n    def tearDownClass(cls):\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.drop_all()\n\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.ctx = app.app_context()\n        self.ctx.push()\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        db.session.rollback()\n        self.ctx.pop()\n\n    def login(self, username='admin', password='adminpass'):\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/login', json={'username': username, 'password': password})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        return resp\n\n    def logout(self):\n        return self.client.post('/api/logout')\n\n    def test_register_and_login(self):\n        # Register new user\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/register', json={\n            'username': 'testuser',\n            'password': 'testpass',\n            'role_id': 1\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('User registered successfully', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Register with existing username\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/register', json={\n            'username': 'testuser',\n            'password': 'anotherpass'\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn('Username already exists', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Register with missing fields\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/register', json={'username': ''})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n\n        # Login with correct credentials\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/login', json={'username': 'testuser', 'password': 'testpass'})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Logged in', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Login with incorrect password\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/login', json={'username': 'testuser', 'password': 'wrong'})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 401)\n        self.assertIn('Invalid credentials', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n    def test_roles_list(self):\n        self.login()\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/roles')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        roles = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(r['name'] == 'admin' for r in roles))\n        self.assertTrue(any(r['name'] == 'accountant' for r in roles))\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_ledger_entry_crud(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add ledger entry\n        data = {\n            'date': '2024-01-01',\n            'account': 'Cash',\n            'description': 'Initial deposit',\n            'debit': 1000,\n            'credit': 0\n        }\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/ledger', json=data)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Entry added', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Add ledger entry with missing fields (should fail)\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/ledger', json={'account': 'Bank'})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n\n        # List ledger entries\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/ledger')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        entries = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(e['account'] == 'Cash' for e in entries))\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_inventory_crud_and_duplicate_sku(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add duplicate SKU\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/inventory', json=data)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn('SKU already exists', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # List inventory items\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/inventory')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        items = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(i['sku'] == 'LAP123' for i in items))\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_purchase_and_inventory_update(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add inventory item\n        item = InventoryItem(name='Monitor', sku='MON123', quantity=5, cost=100, price=150)\n        db.session.add(item)\n        db.session.commit()\n        # Record purchase\n        data = {\n            'date': '2024-01-10',\n            'supplier': 'SupplierA',\n            'total': 200,\n            'items': [{\n                'inventory_item_id': item.id,\n                'quantity': 2,\n                'cost': 100\n            }]\n        }\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/purchases', json=data)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Purchase recorded', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n        # Inventory should be updated\n        updated_item = InventoryItem.query.get(item.id)\n        self.assertEqual(updated_item.quantity, 7)\n        # List purchases\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/purchases')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        purchases = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(p['supplier'] == 'SupplierA' for p in purchases))\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_invoice_and_inventory_update(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add inventory item\n        item = InventoryItem(name='Keyboard', sku='KEY123', quantity=10, cost=20, price=30)\n        db.session.add(item)\n        db.session.commit()\n        # Record invoice\n        data = {\n            'date': '2024-02-01',\n            'customer': 'CustomerA',\n            'total': 60,\n            'items': [{\n                'inventory_item_id': item.id,\n                'quantity': 2,\n                'price': 30\n            }]\n        }\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/invoices', json=data)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Invoice recorded', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n        # Inventory should be reduced\n        updated_item = InventoryItem.query.get(item.id)\n        self.assertEqual(updated_item.quantity, 8)\n        # List invoices\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/invoices')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(i['customer'] == 'CustomerA' for i in invoices))\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_ledger_summary_report(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add ledger entries\n        db.session.add(LedgerEntry(date=datetime(2024, 1, 1), account='Cash', debit=100, credit=0, user_id=self.admin_user.id))\n        db.session.add(LedgerEntry(date=datetime(2024, 1, 2), account='Cash', debit=0, credit=50, user_id=self.admin_user.id))\n        db.session.add(LedgerEntry(date=datetime(2024, 1, 3), account='Bank', debit=200, credit=0, user_id=self.admin_user.id))\n        db.session.commit()\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/reports/ledger-summary')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        summary = resp.get_json()\n        cash_summary = next((s for s in summary if s['account'] == 'Cash'), None)\n        bank_summary = next((s for s in summary if s['account'] == 'Bank'), None)\n        self.assertIsNotNone(cash_summary)\n        self.assertEqual(cash_summary['total_debit'], 100)\n        self.assertEqual(cash_summary['total_credit'], 50)\n        self.assertIsNotNone(bank_summary)\n        self.assertEqual(bank_summary['total_debit'], 200)\n        self.assertEqual(bank_summary['total_credit'], 0)\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_auth_required_for_protected_routes(self):\n        # Try to access protected route without login\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/ledger')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 401)\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/inventory')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 401)\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/purchases')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 401)\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/invoices')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 401)\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/reports/ledger-summary')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 401)\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/roles')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 401)\n\n    def test_logout(self):\n        self.login()\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/logout')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Logged out', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n        # After logout, should not access protected route\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/ledger')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 401)\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    unittest.main()",
                        "import unittest\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom app import app, db, User, Role, InventoryItem, LedgerEntry, Purchase, PurchaseItem, Invoice, InvoiceItem\n\nclass AccountingSystemTestCase(unittest.TestCase):\n    @classmethod\n    def setUpClass(cls):\n        # Use SQLite in-memory DB for testing\n        app.config['SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URI'] = 'sqlite:///:memory:'\n        app.config['TESTING'] = True\n        app.config['WTF_CSRF_ENABLED'] = False\n        app.config['LOGIN_DISABLED'] = False\n        cls.app = app.test_client()\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.create_all()\n            # Create roles\n            admin_role = Role(name='admin')\n            accountant_role = Role(name='accountant')\n            manager_role = Role(name='manager')\n            db.session.add_all([admin_role, accountant_role, manager_role])\n            db.session.commit()\n\n    @classmethod\n    def tearDownClass(cls):\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.session.remove()\n            db.drop_all()\n\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.ctx = app.app_context()\n        self.ctx.push()\n        # Register and login a user for testing\n        self.username = \"testuser\"\n        self.password = \"testpass\"\n        self.role_id = Role.query.filter_by(name='admin').first().id\n        # Register\n        resp = self.app.post('/api/register', json={\n            'username': self.username,\n            'password': self.password,\n            'role_id': self.role_id\n        })\n        # Login\n        resp = self.app.post('/api/login', json={\n            'username': self.username,\n            'password': self.password\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Save session cookie for authenticated requests\n        self.session_cookie = resp.headers.get('Set-Cookie')\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        # Remove all data except roles\n        for model in [User, InventoryItem, LedgerEntry, PurchaseItem, Purchase, InvoiceItem, Invoice]:\n            db.session.query(model).delete()\n        db.session.commit()\n        self.ctx.pop()\n\n    def api_post(self, url, data):\n        return self.app.post(url, json=data, headers={'Cookie': self.session_cookie})\n\n    def api_get(self, url):\n        return self.app.get(url, headers={'Cookie': self.session_cookie})\n\n    # --- User Registration/Login/Logout ---\n\n    def test_register_duplicate_user(self):\n        resp = self.app.post('/api/register', json={\n            'username': self.username,\n            'password': 'anotherpass',\n            'role_id': self.role_id\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn('Username already exists', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n    def test_login_invalid(self):\n        resp = self.app.post('/api/login', json={\n            'username': self.username,\n            'password': 'wrongpass'\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 401)\n        self.assertIn('Invalid credentials', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n    def test_logout(self):\n        resp = self.app.post('/api/logout', headers={'Cookie': self.session_cookie})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Logged out', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n    # --- Roles ---\n\n    def test_get_roles(self):\n        resp = self.api_get('/api/roles')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        roles = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(r['name'] == 'admin' for r in roles))\n        self.assertTrue(any(r['name'] == 'accountant' for r in roles))\n        self.assertTrue(any(r['name'] == 'manager' for r in roles))\n\n    # --- Inventory ---\n\n    def test_inventory_add_and_list(self):\n        # Add item\n        data = {\n            'name': 'Laptop',\n            'sku': 'LAP001',\n            'quantity': 10,\n            'cost': 500.0,\n            'price': 700.0\n        }\n        resp = self.api_post('/api/inventory', data)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Item added', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n        # List items\n        resp = self.api_get('/api/inventory')\n        items = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(items), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(items[0]['name'], 'Laptop')\n        self.assertEqual(items[0]['sku'], 'LAP001')\n        self.assertEqual(items[0]['quantity'], 10)\n\n    def test_inventory_duplicate_sku(self):\n        data = {\n            'name': 'Laptop',\n            'sku': 'LAP001',\n            'quantity': 10,\n            'cost': 500.0,\n            'price': 700.0\n        }\n        resp1 = self.api_post('/api/inventory', data)\n        resp2 = self.api_post('/api/inventory', data)\n        self.assertEqual(resp2.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn('SKU already exists', resp2.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n    # --- Ledger ---\n\n    def test_ledger_add_and_list(self):\n        # Add ledger entry\n        data = {\n            'date': '2024-01-01',\n            'account': 'Cash',\n            'description': 'Initial balance',\n            'debit': 1000.0,\n            'credit': 0.0\n        }\n        resp = self.api_post('/api/ledger', data)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Entry added', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n        # List entries\n        resp = self.api_get('/api/ledger')\n        entries = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(entries), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(entries[0]['account'], 'Cash')\n        self.assertEqual(entries[0]['debit'], 1000.0)\n        self.assertEqual(entries[0]['credit'], 0.0)\n\n    def test_ledger_add_invalid_date(self):\n        data = {\n            'date': 'invalid-date',\n            'account': 'Cash',\n            'description': 'Bad date',\n            'debit': 100.0,\n            'credit': 0.0\n        }\n        resp = self.api_post('/api/ledger', data)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn('Error', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n    # Add purchase\n        data = {\n            'date': '2024-01-02',\n            'supplier': 'Supplier A',\n            'total': 200.0,\n            'items': [\n                {'inventory_item_id': inv.id, 'quantity': 2, 'cost': 100.0}\n            ]\n        }\n        resp = self.api_post('/api/purchases', data)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Purchase recorded', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n        # List purchases\n        resp = self.api_get('/api/purchases')\n        purchases = resp.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(purchases), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(purchases[0]['supplier'], 'Supplier A')\n        self.assertEqual(purchases[0]['items'][0]['quantity'], 2)\n        # Add invoice\n        data = {\n            'date': '2024-01-04',\n            'customer': 'Customer A',\n            'total': 60.0,\n            'items': [\n                {'inventory_item_id': inv.id, 'quantity': 2, 'price': 30.0}\n            ]\n        }\n        resp = self.api_post('/api/invoices', data)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Invoice recorded', resp.get_data(as_text=True))\n        # Should have two accounts\n        accounts = {s['account']: s for s in summary}\n        self.assertIn('Cash', accounts)\n        self.assertIn('Bank', accounts)\n        self.assertEqual(accounts['Cash']['total_debit'], 100.0)\n        self.assertEqual(accounts['Cash']['total_credit'], 50.0)\n        self.assertEqual(accounts['Bank']['total_debit'], 200.0)\n        self.assertEqual(accounts['Bank']['total_credit'], 0.0)\n\n    #                         "import unittest\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom app import app, db, Role, User, InventoryItem, LedgerEntry, Purchase, PurchaseItem, Invoice, InvoiceItem\n\nclass AccountingSystemTestCase(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Use in-memory SQLite for testing\n        app.config['TESTING'] = True\n        app.config['SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URI'] = 'sqlite:///:memory:'\n        app.config['WTF_CSRF_ENABLED'] = False\n        self.app = app.test_client()\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.create_all()\n            # Setup roles\n            admin_role = Role(name='admin')\n            accountant_role = Role(name='accountant')\n            db.session.add_all([admin_role, accountant_role])\n            db.session.commit()\n            # Setup a default user\n            user = User(username='testuser', role_id=admin_role.id)\n            user.set_password('testpass')\n            db.session.add(user)\n            db.session.commit()\n            self.user_id = user.id\n            self.role_id = admin_role.id\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.session.remove()\n            db.drop_all()\n\n    def login(self, username='testuser', password='testpass'):\n        return self.app.post('/api/login', data=json.dumps({\n            'username': username,\n            'password': password\n        }), content_type='application/json')\n\n    def logout(self):\n        return self.app.post('/api/logout')\n\n    def register(self, username, password, role_id=None):\n        data = {'username': username, 'password': password}\n        if role_id:\n            data['role_id'] = role_id\n        return self.app.post('/api/register', data=json.dumps(data), content_type='application/json')\n\n    def test_register_and_login_logout(self):\n        # Register new user\n        rv = self.register('newuser', 'newpass', self.role_id)\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('User registered successfully', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Register with existing username\n        rv = self.register('newuser', 'anotherpass', self.role_id)\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn('Username already exists', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Register with missing fields\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/register', data=json.dumps({'username': ''}), content_type='application/json')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 400)\n\n        # Login with correct credentials\n        rv = self.login('newuser', 'newpass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Logged in', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Login with incorrect credentials\n        rv = self.login('newuser', 'wrongpass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 401)\n        self.assertIn('Invalid credentials', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Login with missing fields\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/login', data=json.dumps({'username': 'newuser'}), content_type='application/json')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 401)\n\n        # Use in-memory SQLite for testing\n        app.config['TESTING'] = True\n        app.config['SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URI'] = 'sqlite:///:memory:'\n        app.config['WTF_CSRF_ENABLED'] = False\n        app.config['LOGIN_DISABLED'] = False\n        self.app = app.test_client()\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.create_all()\n            # Create default roles\n            admin_role = Role(name='admin')\n            accountant_role = Role(name='accountant')\n            manager_role = Role(name='manager')\n            db.session.add_all([admin_role, accountant_role, manager_role])\n            db.session.commit()\n            self.roles = {\n                'admin': admin_role.id,\n                'accountant': accountant_role.id,\n                'manager': manager_role.id\n            }\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.session.remove()\n            db.drop_all()\n\n    def register_user(self, username, password, role_id=None):\n        payload = {'username': username, 'password': password}\n        if role_id:\n            payload['role_id'] = role_id\n        return self.app.post('/api/register', json=payload)\n\n    def login_user(self, username, password):\n        return self.app.post('/api/login', json={'username': username, 'password': password})\n\n    def logout_user(self):\n        return self.app.post('/api/logout')\n\n    def test_register_and_login(self):\n        # Register new user\n        rv = self.register_user('testuser', 'testpass', self.roles['accountant'])\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'User registered successfully', rv.data)\n        # Duplicate username\n        rv2 = self.register_user('testuser', 'testpass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(b'Username already exists', rv2.data)\n        # Login with correct credentials\n        rv3 = self.login_user('testuser', 'testpass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Logged in', rv3.data)\n        # Login with wrong password\n        rv4 = self.login_user('testuser', 'wrongpass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv4.status_code, 401)\n        self.assertIn(b'Invalid credentials', rv4.data)\n        # Login with non-existent user\n        rv5 = self.login_user('nouser', 'pass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv5.status_code, 401)\n        self.assertIn(b'Invalid credentials', rv5.data)\n\n    def login_and_get_cookie(self, username='testuser', password='testpass'):\n        self.register_user(username, password, self.roles['accountant'])\n        rv = self.login_user(username, password)\n        # Get session cookie for authenticated requests\n        cookie = rv.headers.get('Set-Cookie')\n        return cookie\n\n    def auth_headers(self, cookie):\n        return {'Cookie': cookie}\n\n    def test_roles_endpoint(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/roles', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        roles = json.loads(rv.data)\n        self.assertTrue(any(r['name'] == 'admin' for r in roles))\n\n    def test_inventory_crud(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        # Add inventory item\n        item_data = {\n            'name': 'Widget',\n            'sku': 'WGT-001',\n            'quantity': 10,\n            'cost': 5.5,\n            'price': 10.0\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json=item_data, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Item added', rv.data)\n        # Duplicate SKU\n        rv2 = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json=item_data, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(b'SKU already exists', rv2.data)\n        # List inventory\n        rv3 = self.app.get('/api/inventory', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 200)\n        items = json.loads(rv3.data)\n        self.assertEqual(len(items), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(items[0]['sku'], 'WGT-001')\n\n    def test_ledger_entry(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        # Add ledger entry\n        entry_data = {\n            'date': '2024-06-01',\n            'account': 'Cash',\n            'description': 'Initial deposit',\n            'debit': 1000,\n            'credit': 0\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/ledger', json=entry_data, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Entry added', rv.data)\n        # List ledger entries\n        rv2 = self.app.get('/api/ledger', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 200)\n        entries = json.loads(rv2.data)\n        self.assertEqual(len(entries), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(entries[0]['account'], 'Cash')\n        # Edge case: missing date\n        bad_entry = entry_data.copy()\n        bad_entry.pop('date')\n        rv3 = self.app.post('/api/ledger', json=bad_entry, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(b'Error', rv3.data)\n\n    def test_purchases(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        # Add inventory item for purchase\n        item = InventoryItem(name='Widget', sku='WGT-001', quantity=5, cost=5.0, price=10.0)\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.session.add(item)\n            db.session.commit()\n            item_id = item.id\n        purchase_data = {\n            'date': '2024-06-02',\n            'supplier': 'Supplier A',\n            'total': 50.0,\n            'items': [{\n                'inventory_item_id': item_id,\n                'quantity': 10,\n                'cost': 5.0\n            }]\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/purchases', json=purchase_data, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Purchase recorded', rv.data)\n        # List purchases\n        rv2 = self.app.get('/api/purchases', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 200)\n        purchases = json.loads(rv2.data)\n        self.assertEqual(len(purchases), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(purchases[0]['supplier'], 'Supplier A')\n        self.assertEqual(purchases[0]['items'][0]['quantity'], 10)\n        # Inventory quantity should be updated\n        with app.app_context():\n            updated_item = InventoryItem.query.get(item_id)\n            self.assertEqual(updated_item.quantity, 15)\n        # Edge case: missing items\n        bad_purchase = purchase_data.copy()\n        bad_purchase.pop('items')\n        rv3 = self.app.post('/api/purchases', json=bad_purchase, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(b'Error', rv3.data)\n\n    def test_invoices(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        # Add inventory item for invoice\n        item = InventoryItem(name='Gadget', sku='GDT-001', quantity=20, cost=8.0, price=15.0)\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.session.add(item)\n            db.session.commit()\n            item_id = item.id\n        invoice_data = {\n            'date': '2024-06-03',\n            'customer': 'Customer B',\n            'total': 30.0,\n            'items': [{\n                'inventory_item_id': item_id,\n                'quantity': 2,\n                'price': 15.0\n            }]\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/invoices', json=invoice_data, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Invoice recorded', rv.data)\n        # List invoices\n        rv2 = self.app.get('/api/invoices', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = json.loads(rv2.data)\n        self.assertEqual(len(invoices), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(invoices[0]['customer'], 'Customer B')\n        self.assertEqual(invoices[0]['items'][0]['quantity'], 2)\n        # Inventory quantity should be decreased\n        with app.app_context():\n            updated_item = InventoryItem.query.get(item_id)\n            self.assertEqual(updated_item.quantity, 18)\n        # Edge case: missing items\n        bad_invoice = invoice_data.copy()\n        bad_invoice.pop('items')\n        rv3 = self.app.post('/api/invoices', json=bad_invoice, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(b'Error', rv3.data)\n\n    def test_ledger_summary_report(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        # Add ledger entries\n        entries = [\n            {'date': '2024-06-01', 'account': 'Cash', 'description': 'Deposit', 'debit': 1000, 'credit': 0},\n            {'date': '2024-06-02', 'account': 'Cash', 'description': 'Payment', 'debit': 0, 'credit': 200},\n            {'date': '2024-06-02', 'account': 'Sales', 'description': 'Sale', 'debit': 0, 'credit': 300}\n        ]\n        for e in entries:\n            self.app.post('/api/ledger', json=e, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/reports/ledger-summary', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        summary = json.loads(rv.data)\n        cash = next((s for s in summary if s['account'] == 'Cash'), None)\n        sales = next((s for s in summary if s['account'] == 'Sales'), None)\n        self.assertIsNotNone(cash)\n        self.assertEqual(cash['total_debit'], 1000)\n        self.assertEqual(cash['total_credit'], 200)\n        self.assertIsNotNone(sales)\n        self.assertEqual(sales['total_credit'], 300)\n        self.assertEqual(sales['total_debit'], 0)\n\n    def test_logout(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/logout', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Logged out', rv.data)\n\n    def test_protected_routes_require_login(self):\n        # Not logged in, should get 401 or redirect\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/ledger')\n        self.assertIn(rv.status_code, (401, 302))\n        rv2 = self.app.post('/api/ledger', json={})\n        self.assertIn(rv2.status_code, (401, 302))\n        rv3 = self.app.get('/api/inventory')\n        self.assertIn(rv3.status_code, (401, 302))\n\n    def test_invalid_methods(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        # Try PUT on inventory (not allowed)\n        rv = self.app.put('/api/inventory', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 405)\n        # Try DELETE on ledger (not allowed)\n        rv2 = self.app.delete('/api/ledger', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 405)\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    unittest.main()",

                        "import unittest\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom app import app, db, Role, User, InventoryItem, LedgerEntry, Purchase, PurchaseItem, Invoice, InvoiceItem\n\nclass AccountingSystemTestCase(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Use in-memory SQLite for tests\n        app.config['TESTING'] = True\n        app.config['SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URI'] = 'sqlite:///:memory:'\n        app.config['WTF_CSRF_ENABLED'] = False\n        app.config['LOGIN_DISABLED'] = False\n        self.app = app.test_client()\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.create_all()\n            # Create roles\n            admin_role = Role(name='admin')\n            accountant_role = Role(name='accountant')\n            manager_role = Role(name='manager')\n            db.session.add_all([admin_role, accountant_role, manager_role])\n            db.session.commit()\n            self.roles = {\n                'admin': admin_role,\n                'accountant': accountant_role,\n                'manager': manager_role\n            }\n            # Register with new username\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/register', json={'username': 'newuser', 'password': 'newpass'})\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('User registered successfully', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n    def test_login_logout(self):\n        # Wrong credentials\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/login', json={'username': 'testuser', 'password': 'wrongpass'})\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 401)\n        self.assertIn('Invalid credentials', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Correct credentials\n        rv = self.login()\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Logged in', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Logout\n        rv = self.logout()\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Logged out', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n    def test_roles_list(self):\n        self.login()\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/roles')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        roles = rv.get_json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(r['name'] == 'admin' for r in roles))\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_inventory_crud(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add item\n        data = {\n            'name': 'Laptop',\n            'sku': 'SKU123',\n            'quantity': 10,\n            'cost': 500,\n            'price': 700\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json=data)\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Item added', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Add duplicate SKU\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json=data)\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn('SKU already exists', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # List items\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/inventory')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        items = rv.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(items), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(items[0]['sku'], 'SKU123')\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_ledger_entry(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add ledger entry\n        data = {\n            'date': '2024-06-01',\n            'account': 'Cash',\n            'description': 'Initial capital',\n            'debit': 1000,\n            'credit': 0\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/ledger', json=data)\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Entry added', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Add entry with missing date\n        bad_data = dict(data)\n        del bad_data['date']\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/ledger', json=bad_data)\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn('Error', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # List ledger entries\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/ledger')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        entries = rv.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(entries), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(entries[0]['account'], 'Cash')\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_purchases(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add inventory item first\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json={\n            'name': 'Monitor',\n            'sku': 'SKU456',\n            'quantity': 5,\n            'cost': 100,\n            'price': 150\n        })\n        item_id = InventoryItem.query.filter_by(sku='SKU456').first().id\n\n        # Record purchase\n        data = {\n            'date': '2024-06-02',\n            'supplier': 'SupplierA',\n            'total': 200,\n            'items': [\n                {'inventory_item_id': item_id, 'quantity': 2, 'cost': 100}\n            ]\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/purchases', json=data)\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Purchase recorded', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # List purchases\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/purchases')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        purchases = rv.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(purchases), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(purchases[0]['supplier'], 'SupplierA')\n\n        # Edge case: purchase with invalid inventory item\n        bad_data = dict(data)\n        bad_data['items'] = [{'inventory_item_id': 9999, 'quantity': 1, 'cost': 100}]\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/purchases', json=bad_data)\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)  # Should still succeed, but not update inventory\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_invoices(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add inventory item first\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json={\n            'name': 'Keyboard',\n            'sku': 'SKU789',\n            'quantity': 10,\n            'cost': 20,\n            'price': 35\n        })\n        item_id = InventoryItem.query.filter_by(sku='SKU789').first().id\n\n        # Record invoice\n        data = {\n            'date': '2024-06-03',\n            'customer': 'CustomerA',\n            'total': 70,\n            'items': [\n                {'inventory_item_id': item_id, 'quantity': 2, 'price': 35}\n            ]\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/invoices', json=data)\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn('Invoice recorded', rv.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # List invoices\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/invoices')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = rv.get_json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(invoices), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(invoices[0]['customer'], 'CustomerA')\n\n        # Edge case: invoice with invalid inventory item\n        bad_data = dict(data)\n        bad_data['items'] = [{'inventory_item_id': 9999, 'quantity': 1, 'price': 35}]\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/invoices', json=bad_data)\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)  # Should still succeed, but not update inventory\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_ledger_summary_report(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add multiple ledger entries\n        entries = [\n            {'date': '2024-06-01', 'account': 'Cash', 'debit': 1000, 'credit': 0},\n            {'date': '2024-06-02', 'account': 'Sales', 'debit': 0, 'credit': 500},\n            {'date': '2024-06-03', 'account': 'Cash', 'debit': 200, 'credit': 0},\n            {'date': '2024-06-04', 'account': 'Sales', 'debit': 0, 'credit': 300}\n        ]\n        for entry in entries:\n            entry['description'] = 'Test'\n            self.app.post('/api/ledger', json=entry)\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/reports/ledger-summary')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        summary = rv.get_json()\n        # Check that both accounts are present\n        accounts = {s['account']: s for s in summary}\n        self.assertIn('Cash', accounts)\n        self.assertEqual(accounts['Cash']['total_debit'], 1200)\n        self.assertEqual(accounts['Cash']['total_credit'], 0)\n        self.assertIn('Sales', accounts)\n        self.assertEqual(accounts['Sales']['total_debit'], 0)\n        self.assertEqual(accounts['Sales']['total_credit'], 800)\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_access_control(self):\n        # Access protected route without login\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/ledger')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 401)  # Unauthorized\n\n        # Login and access\n        self.login()\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/ledger')\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_inventory_edge_cases(self):\n        self.login()\n        # Add item with zero quantity, cost, price\n        data = {\n            'name': 'ZeroItem',\n            'sku': 'SKUZERO',\n            'quantity': 0,\n            'cost': 0,\n            'price': 0\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json=data)\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        items = self.app.get('/api/inventory').get_json()\n        zero_item = next(i for i in items if i['sku'] == 'SKUZERO')\n        self.assertEqual(zero_item['quantity'], 0)\n        self.assertEqual(zero_item['cost'], 0)\n        self.assertEqual(zero_item['price'], 0)\n        self.logout()\n\n    def test_serve_frontend(self):\n        # Duplicate username\n        rv2 = self.register_user('testuser', 'testpass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(b'Username already exists', rv2.data)\n        # Login with correct credentials\n        rv3 = self.login_user('testuser', 'testpass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Logged in', rv3.data)\n        # Login with wrong password\n        rv4 = self.login_user('testuser', 'wrongpass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv4.status_code, 401)\n        self.assertIn(b'Invalid credentials', rv4.data)\n        # Login with non-existent user\n        rv5 = self.login_user('nouser', 'pass')\n        self.assertEqual(rv5.status_code, 401)\n        self.assertIn(b'Invalid credentials', rv5.data)\n\n    def login_and_get_cookie(self, username='testuser', password='testpass'):\n        self.register_user(username, password, self.roles['accountant'])\n        rv = self.login_user(username, password)\n        # Get session cookie for authenticated requests\n        cookie = rv.headers.get('Set-Cookie')\n        return cookie\n\n    def auth_headers(self, cookie):\n        return {'Cookie': cookie}\n\n    def test_roles_endpoint(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/roles', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        roles = json.loads(rv.data)\n        self.assertTrue(any(r['name'] == 'admin' for r in roles))\n\n    def test_inventory_crud(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        # Add inventory item\n        item_data = {\n            'name': 'Widget',\n            'sku': 'WGT-001',\n            'quantity': 10,\n            'cost': 5.5,\n            'price': 10.0\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json=item_data, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Item added', rv.data)\n        # Duplicate SKU\n        rv2 = self.app.post('/api/inventory', json=item_data, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(b'SKU already exists', rv2.data)\n        # List inventory\n        rv3 = self.app.get('/api/inventory', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 200)\n        items = json.loads(rv3.data)\n        self.assertEqual(len(items), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(items[0]['sku'], 'WGT-001')\n\n    def test_ledger_entry(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        # Add ledger entry\n        entry_data = {\n            'date': '2024-06-01',\n            'account': 'Cash',\n            'description': 'Initial deposit',\n            'debit': 1000,\n            'credit': 0\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/ledger', json=entry_data, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Entry added', rv.data)\n        # List ledger entries\n        rv2 = self.app.get('/api/ledger', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 200)\n        entries = json.loads(rv2.data)\n        self.assertEqual(len(entries), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(entries[0]['account'], 'Cash')\n        # Edge case: missing date\n        bad_entry = entry_data.copy()\n        bad_entry.pop('date')\n        rv3 = self.app.post('/api/ledger', json=bad_entry, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(b'Error', rv3.data)\n\n    def test_purchases(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        # Add inventory item for purchase\n        item = InventoryItem(name='Widget', sku='WGT-001', quantity=5, cost=5.0, price=10.0)\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.session.add(item)\n            db.session.commit()\n            item_id = item.id\n        purchase_data = {\n            'date': '2024-06-02',\n            'supplier': 'Supplier A',\n            'total': 50.0,\n            'items': [{\n                'inventory_item_id': item_id,\n                'quantity': 10,\n                'cost': 5.0\n            }]\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/purchases', json=purchase_data, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Purchase recorded', rv.data)\n        # List purchases\n        rv2 = self.app.get('/api/purchases', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 200)\n        purchases = json.loads(rv2.data)\n        self.assertEqual(len(purchases), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(purchases[0]['supplier'], 'Supplier A')\n        self.assertEqual(purchases[0]['items'][0]['quantity'], 10)\n        # Inventory quantity should be updated\n        with app.app_context():\n            updated_item = InventoryItem.query.get(item_id)\n            self.assertEqual(updated_item.quantity, 15)\n        # Edge case: missing items\n        bad_purchase = purchase_data.copy()\n        bad_purchase.pop('items')\n        rv3 = self.app.post('/api/purchases', json=bad_purchase, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(b'Error', rv3.data)\n\n    def test_invoices(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        # Add inventory item for invoice\n        item = InventoryItem(name='Gadget', sku='GDT-001', quantity=20, cost=8.0, price=15.0)\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.session.add(item)\n            db.session.commit()\n            item_id = item.id\n        invoice_data = {\n            'date': '2024-06-03',\n            'customer': 'Customer B',\n            'total': 30.0,\n            'items': [{\n                'inventory_item_id': item_id,\n                'quantity': 2,\n                'price': 15.0\n            }]\n        }\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/invoices', json=invoice_data, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Invoice recorded', rv.data)\n        # List invoices\n        rv2 = self.app.get('/api/invoices', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = json.loads(rv2.data)\n        self.assertEqual(len(invoices), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(invoices[0]['customer'], 'Customer B')\n        self.assertEqual(invoices[0]['items'][0]['quantity'], 2)\n        # Inventory quantity should be decreased\n        with app.app_context():\n            updated_item = InventoryItem.query.get(item_id)\n            self.assertEqual(updated_item.quantity, 18)\n        # Edge case: missing items\n        bad_invoice = invoice_data.copy()\n        bad_invoice.pop('items')\n        rv3 = self.app.post('/api/invoices', json=bad_invoice, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv3.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(b'Error', rv3.data)\n\n    def test_ledger_summary_report(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        # Add ledger entries\n        entries = [\n            {'date': '2024-06-01', 'account': 'Cash', 'description': 'Deposit', 'debit': 1000, 'credit': 0},\n            {'date': '2024-06-02', 'account': 'Cash', 'description': 'Payment', 'debit': 0, 'credit': 200},\n            {'date': '2024-06-02', 'account': 'Sales', 'description': 'Sale', 'debit': 0, 'credit': 300}\n        ]\n        for e in entries:\n            self.app.post('/api/ledger', json=e, headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/reports/ledger-summary', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        summary = json.loads(rv.data)\n        cash = next((s for s in summary if s['account'] == 'Cash'), None)\n        sales = next((s for s in summary if s['account'] == 'Sales'), None)\n        self.assertIsNotNone(cash)\n        self.assertEqual(cash['total_debit'], 1000)\n        self.assertEqual(cash['total_credit'], 200)\n        self.assertIsNotNone(sales)\n        self.assertEqual(sales['total_credit'], 300)\n        self.assertEqual(sales['total_debit'], 0)\n\n    def test_logout(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        rv = self.app.post('/api/logout', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(b'Logged out', rv.data)\n\n    def test_protected_routes_require_login(self):\n        # Not logged in, should get 401 or redirect\n        rv = self.app.get('/api/ledger')\n        self.assertIn(rv.status_code, (401, 302))\n        rv2 = self.app.post('/api/ledger', json={})\n        self.assertIn(rv2.status_code, (401, 302))\n        rv3 = self.app.get('/api/inventory')\n        self.assertIn(rv3.status_code, (401, 302))\n\n    def test_invalid_methods(self):\n        cookie = self.login_and_get_cookie()\n        # Try PUT on inventory (not allowed)\n        rv = self.app.put('/api/inventory', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv.status_code, 405)\n        # Try DELETE on ledger (not allowed)\n        rv2 = self.app.delete('/api/ledger', headers=self.auth_headers(cookie))\n        self.assertEqual(rv2.status_code, 405)\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    unittest.main()",
